 Many times you must have also performed this jaikaara, but have you ever thought that why do they apply this jaikaara? Where did this cheer originate? The roots of this Ganpati cheer 21 km from Pune in Maharashtra
 dur based chinchvaad gaanv main hai
 Chinchwad is the birthplace of a saint whose devotion and faith has written a story, after which the name of Ganapati was also added to his name
 pandravi shatabdi main ek sant hue, jinka naam tha morya gosaavi
 It is said that Morya Gosavi was born with the blessings of Lord Ganesha and Morya Gosavi also worshiped Lord Ganesha like his parents
 har saal ganesh chaturthi ke shubh avasar par morya chinchvaad se morgaanv ganesh kii puja karne ke liye paidal jaaya karte the
 It is said that due to growing age one day Lord Ganesha himself came in his dream and told him that his idol will be found in the river
 or thik vaisaa hi hua, nadi main snaan ke dauraan unhen ganesh ji kii murti mili
 After this incident people started believing that if there is any devotee of Ganapati Bappa, then he is only and only Morya Gosavi
 tabhi se bhakt chinchvaad gaanv main morya gosaavi ke darshan ke liye aane lage
 It is said that when devotees used to touch Morya by touching the feet of Gosavi ji and Saint Morya used to say Mangalmurti to his devotees and then started Mangalamurthy Morya
 jo jayakaara pune ke paas chinchvaad gaanv se shuru hua wo jayakaara aaj ganpati bappa ke har bhakt ke jubaan par he
 But as far as the public event of Ganapati Puja is concerned, it was started by freedom fighter Balgangadhar Lokmanya Tilak
 morya gosaavi mandir main saal main do baar vishesh utsav kaa aayojan kiya jaataa he
 One is in the month of Bhadrapada and the second in the month of Magh, when the palanquin comes out of the temple, which is taken to the Ganapati temple of Morgaon for darshan
